#  [](/thread/38542-pivot-point-with-money-management-strategy)Pivot Point with Money Management Strategy 

  * 

  * [#1](/thread/38542-pivot-point-with-money-management-strategy "Post Permalink")

  * First Post: Edited Jul 17, 2007 12:52pm  Jul 16, 2007 6:41pm | Edited Jul 17, 2007 12:52pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41068_4.gif) Olaha](olaha)

  * | Joined Jun 2007  | Status: Leading Trader | [399 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41068)

I assume everybody knows how to enter and exit the market but don't know a few rules that related to Money management.  
  
Such as;  
  
i - where to enter & exit with Money management,  
ii- where to display stop loss with Money management,  
iii- how to diversify the account with Money management (Scale),  
iv- how much we can risk our account.  
  
The website for Pivot Point;  
[http://www.actionforex.com/forex_ana..._200603215756/](http://www.actionforex.com/forex_analysis_and_forecasts/pivot_points/gbpusd_200603215756/)  
  
  
1) Where to enter & Exit;  
  
Everybody has own way of enter in to the market. No body can say the way you enter the trade is wrong. But, it's depend on how long you want to hold the market if the time that you enter the trade is non active market.  
  
The best time to enter the trades are during London Session and New York session.  
  
Once we know when is the best time to trade, we should know what is the trend for the day. The easy way to find the direction of the trend for the days is using the Pivot Point (PP). If the opening price is above the PP means Bullish. If the opening price is below the PP means Bearish.  
  
Now we have to find out what price to enter. Using the PP level at Daily, 4 hours, hourly will help us to place an entry.  
  
Entry Strategy;  
  
If the price above the PP level Daily, 4 hrs, hourly, we can enter at R1 hourly PP.  
  
If the price below the PP level Daily, 4 hrs, hourly, we can enter at S1 hourly PP.  
................................................  
The most difficult part is where to exit. We always say, we want to let the profit run until maximum level. How do we know the maximum level?. The PP will came-in as a leading indicator. This is one of the way we can discipline ourself.  
  
Exit Strategy;  
  
For buy - use 4 hours PP level (R1,R2,R3) for exit level,  
For sell - use 4 hours PP level (S1,S2,S3) for exit level.  
  
2). Where to display stop loss;  
  
Before we can start trading our money into the market, We should ask ourself. How much we willing to lost. We can use PP to display the Stop Loss (SL).  
  
There are 2 way we can place the SL;  
  
a). If the entry using 4 hrs than the SL also at 4 hrs PP,  
b). If the entry using hourly than the SL also at hourly PP.  
  
When the price reach at R2/S2 level, the SL will move to R1/S1 and so on..  
  
3). How to diversify the account (Scale);  
  
This is the most important part of Money Management. I like to name it as a scale strategy. Scale strategy can be use in any range of market. I realise that this method help a lot on to diversity our account with affective and efficient.  
  
For Mini Account;  
1 lot = 10 units  
or  
1 lot = 100 units  
  
For Normal Account;  
1 lot = 1000 units;  
or  
1 lot = 10,000 units  
  
The strategy;  
For Bullish, look for the range from R1 to R3, or  
For Bearish, look for the range from S1 to S3  
  
Example 1:  
  
Let's say the range between R1 to R3 or S1 to S3 (4 hrs pivot) is 40.  
  
So we can do scalling to 2 target;  
1st target at 20 pips, the 2nd target at 20 pips.  
  
We plan for this range with 1 lot for every 20 pips;  
It's mean, We can buy 2 lots.  
1st lot close 20 pips at target 1,  
2nd lot close 20 pips at target 2  
  
Take your profit every 20 pips move. Every 20 pips take 1 lot. Once the 1st profit taken, move the SL at break even (b/e) or +3.  
  
For the range 50 or 60;  
Scale = 20/20/10 or 20/20/20 (3 lots)  
(SL move to b/e after 1st lot taken, after the 2nd lots taken, move the SL at target 1.)  
  
For the range 70 or 80;  
Scale = 20/20/20/10 or 20/20/20/20 (4 lots)  
(SL move to b/e after 1st lot taken, after the 2nd lots taken, move the SL at target 1 price, than when the 3rd lots taken move the SL at target 2)  
  
For the range 90 or 100;  
Scale =20/20/20/20/10 or 20/20/20/20/20 (5 lots)  
(SL move to b/e after 1st lot taken, after the 2nd lots taken, move the SL at target 1 price, than when the 3rd lots taken move the SL at target 2, after the 4th lots take move the SL at target 3)  
  
4). How much we can risk our account;  
  
We should know the size of our account that available for us to trade.  
The Ratio that suitable for each trader also different.   
For those still in mini account, try to use ratio 1:1 or 5:1  
For those experience trader can use 10:1 or 50:1  
  
Use this calculator, to find out how much the size of account that we can expose.  
  
[http://www.oanda.com/products/fxmath...vailable.shtml](http://www.oanda.com/products/fxmath/units_available.shtml)  
  
5). Technical Indicator;  
  
Try to use 2 to 3 Technical Indicator only.   
Stochastic 14,3,3 + EMA14 (plot EMA 14 inside the Stochastic 14,3,3)  
This indicator use to looking for retracement.  
  
How to use the Stochastic?  
Use this Stochastic to see the retracement level.  
Look for new cross.  
  
For bullish;  
Try to take new cross from below 50 level to upward.  
If the cross happen at above 50 to upward, the bullish continue but not that big move. This can be use as a signal for overbought.  
  
For bearish;  
Try to take new cross from above 50 level to downward.  
If the cross happen at below 50 level to downward, the bearish continue but not that big move. This can be as a signal for oversold.  
  
How stochastic work with EMA14?  
When the stochastic cross with EMA14, this can be a 2nd confirmation for entry and exit.  
  
At chart 15 minutes.  
  
The looks will be like this;

Yes only Stoch 14,3,3 + EMA14.  
You can mix with any indicator that suite you.   
But try not to use more than 3 technical indicators.  
If too much indicator, you will get confuse.  
Try to use system that simple as much you can.  
  
How to use the Stochastic?  
Use this Stochastic to see the retracement level.   
Look for new cross.   
  
For bullish;  
Try to take new cross from below 50 level to upward.  
If the cross happen at above 50 to upward, the bullish continue but not that big move. This can be use as a signal for overbought.  
  
For bearish;  
Try to take new cross from above 50 level to downward.  
If the cross happen at below 50 level to downward, the bearish continue but not that big move. This can be as a signal for oversold.  
  
How stochastic work with EMA14?  
When the stochastic cross with EMA14, this can be a 2nd confirmation for entry and exit.  
  
I hope this will help you and others to be a smarter trader.  
  
Good Luck! ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f44d.png?v=15.1)

#  [](/thread/38542-pivot-point-with-money-management-strategy)Pivot Point with Money Management Strategy 

  *

Seem you doing great.. 117 pips.   
  
I give some tips for you, how to be discipline;  
1). Wake-up in the morning, same time every day,  
2). Sleep also at the same time every day,  
3). Eat also at the same time every day,  
4). Take a bath also the same time every day.  
5). Exercise at the same time every day (15 minutes).  
  
Practice those for 1 week. If you can do those, you will manage to follow your own rule of trading.   
  
As I mention earlier, if you can discipline yourself in routine/daily life... we can discipline ourself in trading also.  
  
Good Luck!

I trade news after 5 minutes on release time. The spread is big (15-20 spread). So, I wait until the spread back to normal (2.5).   
  
If I am very sure on the direction for the day, I will place an order.  
  
Off course is good time to trade news...but if the price goes to wrong direction, you will loss the account. Sometimes.. I take the risk.  
  
For those new trader, try avoid news release.

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41068_4.gif) Olaha](olaha)

  * | Joined Jun 2007  | Status: Leading Trader | [399 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41068)

I like to use few time frame to find out the retracement. I use 1 hour and 15 minutes. The 1 hour can show a the the end of trend. Normally I look for the stochastic to reach 90 level and cross. That is the sign of retracement. Than I look for short time frame to see if they are any new cross at the bottom to take for bullish bias. Don't worry... you have to study a lot of pattern than you understand. Take your time. While you trade with me, you will learn more. Make sure, take some notes every time you find a new things. That's how I started.

  * [#70](/thread/post/1498295#post1498295 "Post Permalink")

  * Jul 18, 2007 2:44pm  Jul 18, 2007 2:44pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41068_4.gif) Olaha](olaha)

  * | Joined Jun 2007  | Status: Leading Trader | [399 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41068)

Ammendment  

> [Quoting Olaha](/thread/post/1495763#post1495763 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> I assume everybody knows how to enter and exit the market but don't know a few rules that related to Money management.  
>    
>  Such as;  
>    
>  i - where to enter & exit with Money management,  
>  ii- where to display stop loss with Money management,  
>  iii- how to diversify the account with Money management (Scale),  
>  iv- how much we can risk our account.  
>    
>  The website for Pivot Point;  
>  [http://www.actionforex.com/forex_ana..._200603215756/](http://www.actionforex.com/forex_analysis_and_forecasts/pivot_points/gbpusd_200603215756/)  
>    
>    
>  1) Where to enter & Exit;  
>    
>  Everybody has own way of enter in to the market. No body can say the way you enter the trade is wrong. But, it's depend on how long you want to hold the market if the time that you enter the trade is non active market.  
>    
>  The best time to enter the trades are during London Session and New York session.  
>    
>  Once we know when is the best time to trade, we should know what is the trend for the day. The easy way to find the direction of the trend for the days is using the Pivot Point (PP). If the opening price is above the PP means Bullish. If the opening price is below the PP means Bearish.  
>    
>  Now we have to find out what price to enter. Using the PP level at Daily, 4 hours, hourly will help us to place an entry.  
>    
>  Entry Strategy;  
>    
>  If the price above the PP level Daily, 4 hrs, hourly, we can enter at R1 hourly PP.  
>    
>  If the price below the PP level Daily, 4 hrs, hourly, we can enter at S1 hourly PP.  
>  ................................................  
>  The most difficult part is where to exit. We always say, we want to let the profit run until maximum level. How do we know the maximum level?. The PP will came-in as a leading indicator. This is one of the way we can discipline ourself.  
>    
>  Exit Strategy;  
>    
>  For buy - use 4 hours PP level (R1,R2,R3) for exit level,  
>  For sell - use 4 hours PP level (S1,S2,S3) for exit level.  
>    
>  2). Where to display stop loss;  
>    
>  Before we can start trading our money into the market, We should ask ourself. How much we willing to lost. We can use PP to display the Stop Loss (SL).  
>    
>  There are 2 way we can place the SL;  
>    
>  a). If the entry using 4 hrs than the SL also at 4 hrs PP,  
>  b). If the entry using hourly than the SL also at hourly PP.  
>    
>  When the price reach at R2/S2 level, the SL will move to R1/S1 and so on..  
>    
>  3). How to diversify the account (Scale);  
>    
>  This is the most important part of Money Management. I like to name it as a scale strategy. Scale strategy can be use in any range of market. I realise that this method help a lot on to diversity our account with affective and efficient.  
>    
>  For Mini Account;  
>  1 lot = 10 units  
>  or  
>  1 lot = 100 units  
>    
>  For Normal Account;  
>  1 lot = 1000 units;  
>  or  
>  1 lot = 10,000 units  
>    
>  The strategy;  
>  For Bullish, look for the range from R1 to R3, or  
>  For Bearish, look for the range from S1 to S3  
>    
>  Example 1:  
>    
>  Let's say the range between R1 to R3 or S1 to S3 (4 hrs pivot) is 40.  
>    
>  So we can do scalling to 2 target;  
>  1st target at 20 pips, the 2nd target at 20 pips.  
>    
>  We plan for this range with 1 lot for every 20 pips;  
>  It's mean, We can buy 2 lots.  
>  1st lot close 20 pips at target 1,  
>  2nd lot close 20 pips at target 2  
>    
>  Take your profit every 20 pips move. Every 20 pips take 1 lot. Once the 1st profit taken, move the SL at break even (b/e) or +3.  
>    
>  For the range 50 or 60;  
>  Scale = 20/20/10 or 20/20/20 (3 lots)  
>  (SL move to b/e after 1st lot taken, after the 2nd lots taken, move the SL at target 1.)  
>    
>  For the range 70 or 80;  
>  Scale = 20/20/20/10 or 20/20/20/20 (4 lots)  
>  (SL move to b/e after 1st lot taken, after the 2nd lots taken, move the SL at target 1 price, than when the 3rd lots taken move the SL at target 2)  
>    
>  For the range 90 or 100;  
>  Scale =20/20/20/20/10 or 20/20/20/20/20 (5 lots)  
>  (SL move to b/e after 1st lot taken, after the 2nd lots taken, move the SL at target 1 price, than when the 3rd lots taken move the SL at target 2, after the 4th lots take move the SL at target 3)  
>    
>  4). How much we can risk our account;  
>    
>  We should know the size of our account that available for us to trade.  
>  The Ratio that suitable for each trader also different.   
>  For those still in mini account, try to use ratio 1:1 or 5:1  
>  For those experience trader can use 10:1 or 50:1  
>    
>  Use this calculator, to find out how much the size of account that we can expose.  
>    
>  [http://www.oanda.com/products/fxmath...vailable.shtml](http://www.oanda.com/products/fxmath/units_available.shtml)  
>    
>  5). Technical Indicator;  
>    
>  Try to use 2 to 3 Technical Indicator only.   
>  For 1 hour chart - Stochastic 14,3,3 + EMA14 (plot EMA 14 inside the Stochastic 14,3,3)  
>    
>  For 15 minutes chart -Stochastic 5,3,3 + EMA5  
>    
>  This indicator use to looking for retracement.  
>    
>  How to use the Stochastic?  
>  Use this Stochastic to see the retracement level.  
>  Look for new cross.  
>    
>  For bullish;  
>  Try to take new cross from below 50 level to upward.  
>  If the cross happen at above 50 to upward, the bullish continue but not that big move. This can be use as a signal for overbought.  
>    
>  For bearish;  
>  Try to take new cross from above 50 level to downward.  
>  If the cross happen at below 50 level to downward, the bearish continue but not that big move. This can be as a signal for oversold.  
>    
>  How stochastic work with EMA14?  
>  When the stochastic cross with EMA14, this can be a 2nd confirmation for entry and exit.  
>    
>  At chart 15 minutes.  
>    
>  The looks will be like this;
> 
> Ignored

At 10 a.m. NY time we have Bernanke talking and giving his semiannual testimony. Everybody expects him to be hawkish, and if he drops his hawkish tone, I think we may possibly see GBP/USD gain 50 pips or more in the first hour of the report. If you are new to this, I suggest you to skip the testimony because it may be a little bit too tricky.

  * [#114](/thread/post/1501582#post1501582 "Post Permalink")

  * Jul 20, 2007 5:17pm  Jul 20, 2007 5:17pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41068_4.gif) Olaha](olaha)

  * | Joined Jun 2007  | Status: Leading Trader | [399 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41068)

Actually is very simple rule that you should follow;  
  
Look for PP level for Daily, 4 hrs, hourly.  
If the price is above the Pivot for Daily, 4 hrs and hourly =bullish  
If the price is below the Pivot for Daily, 4 hrs and hourly =bearish  
  
The entry at R1 for buy/ S1 for Sell (4 hrs PP)  
SL will be at Pivot level for either buy or sell.  
With confirmation from Stochastic.  
  
I think... you need to read again on page 1 of this thread to get better understanding.

  * [#116](/thread/post/1501618#post1501618 "Post Permalink")

  * Jul 20, 2007 5:38pm  Jul 20, 2007 5:38pm 

  * [ vasyan](vasyan)

  * | Joined May 2006  | Status: Trader | [29 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=10573)

It depends on what is counted as a lot\or unit .. Say when i sell\buy 1 lot through my broker i sell\buy $1k ( 1 pp = $0.1, 4 lots -> 1pp=$0.4 and so on.. )  
  
As to the rules.. I see it the following way  
  
If the day open above a pivot, then set an enter around a pivot ( the price always runs to pivot prior to moving to R1 etc. Watch some days for it and you'll see it's true 90% of time)  
SL - under S1  
  
R\R ratio is 1:1 in this case, with the possibility to rise higher..  
  
More profitable is such a case :  
  
If the price crossed the pivot not reaching 1st R or S - then it 99% will reach opposite S or R **3** (respectively)  
Say it opened under the pivot, fell a bit but did not reach the S1 then went up above a pivot (and it happened at the past part of eu session, not earlier) - it always goes to #3 level in such cases .. That's all 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

  * [#117](/thread/post/1501672#post1501672 "Post Permalink")

  * Jul 20, 2007 5:59pm  Jul 20, 2007 5:59pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41068_4.gif) Olaha](olaha)

  * | Joined Jun 2007  | Status: Leading Trader | [399 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41068)

As what I always mention, the entry at R1 or S1 but I don't enter on the spot... I always remind to wait for retracement to get confirmation. If the price came back to Pivot means no trade. But if the price been to R1/S1 and retrace above the pivot than came back again to R1/S1.. the price will not came back to Pivot level again. Because the price always test the strength at R1/S1 level. If the price agree than the price will continue to go to R2 and R3 or S2 and S3 (4 hours PP).  
  
I hope this will convince you....

  * | Joined Jun 2007  | Status: Leading Trader | [399 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41068)

This information may help everybody to see the history for today's trade as a lesson;  
  
7GMT;  
R1=2.0495  
P=2.0487  
  
The price already tested on R1 level =2.0495  
  
7.15GMT;  
Price retrace at P level.  
So, No entry  
  
8GMT;  
R1=2.0495  
P =2.0487  
  
8GMT;  
Price test again at R1,  
  
8.15 GMT;  
Price fail to retrace at P level  
  
8.30 GMT;  
Place order at R1 = 2.0495 - 2.0521  
(Can use 1 hour PP level as Alternative)  
Entry at R1=2.0495  
SL =2.0487  
  
9GMT;  
R1 = 2.0513 (R3=2.0540)  
P=2.0499  
  
We can move our take profit level at R3=2.0540  
New SL = 2.0499  
  
9.45GMT;  
Profit taken at R3 = 2.0540  
  
Profit for the day = 45 pips

I am happy to hear that you can follow the system.  
Normally the price will not follow the range at 4H because the big move happen during the news release. So we have to look for Daily range.  
During the news release.. esp. during major news, I try to take short term trades. Not more than 30 minutes, because anything can be happen during the 1 hr period. Once everybody take out profit, the price can reverse.   
I hope this answer may help you for the future decision.  
  
Good Luck!

  * [#148](/thread/post/1549931#post1549931 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 21, 2007 5:24pm  Aug 21, 2007 5:24pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41068_4.gif) Olaha](olaha)

  * | Joined Jun 2007  | Status: Leading Trader | [399 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41068)

Dear Steven,  
  
Thank you for your question.  
Please don't confuse...  
  
The answer for your question;  
To enter the market either buy or sell is depends on the PP level.  
  
If the price above the PP level for daily... bullish  
price below the PP level for daily...bearish  
  
When we know either bullish or bearish...  
than we have to wait until the price retest the R1 for buy,  
S1 for sell. (4 hrs or 1 hr Pivot)  
  
After the price retest the R1 for buy or S1 for sell - make sure the price doesn't retrace at Pivot level.  
  
If the price doesn't retrace the Pivel level than we enter at R1 for buy and S1 for sell.  
  
If the price retrace at Pivot level than wait for next retracement.  
  
Try not to use this system during the news release.  
  
I hope this explanation may help you.  
  
Let me know if you do not understand.  
  
Good Luck! 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

Okay. So suppose you start at 6:45 EST (15m candle - open 1.9817)  
  
Daily PP - 1.9847  
4h PP - 1.9814  
Hourly PP - 1.9797  
  
Would you conisder this bearish since its below the Daily Pivot? Or would you just not trade this until the Price was either below or above all the pivot points for a stronger sense of trend? 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

  * [#153](/thread/post/1550267#post1550267 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 21, 2007 8:23pm  Aug 21, 2007 8:23pm 

  * [ S-Deuce](s-deuce)

  * | Joined Jul 2007  | Status: Trader | [75 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=42853)

Another thing - When you are talking about scaling and taking profits every 20 pips....  
  
Say the range from R1 to R3 is 40 pips. Lets use R1 = 1.9800 R2 = 1.9820 R3 = 1.9840.  
  
Do you:  
a) buy 2 lots when you enter the market at 1.9800? Then close 1 lot at 1.9820 (20 pip profit) then close the 2nd lot at 1.9840 (40 pip profit)?   
b) buy 1 lot at 1.9800 and close it out at 1.9820 then buy another lot at 1.9820 and set your SL at 1.9800 and take profit at 1.9840?  
  
If it is (b) then how do you know the market will keep going up? You just keep going til it stops you out? 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

If you look at hourly...  
You could enter buy at R1 - 1.9817 and take profit at 1.9853  
The price tested at R1 than retrace at 1.9810.  
This is the good example for short term trade.

  * Aug 22, 2007 4:11pm  Aug 22, 2007 4:11pm 

  * [ gtketum](gtketum)

  * | Joined Oct 2006  | Status: Trader | [68 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=21048)

so based on this, let me see if i can call the trades and please correct me if im wrong on this.   
  
right now the price is around 1.9850  
  
it is clearly above all pivot points.   
  
4 hr PP = 1.9819 and R1 = 1.9833. so if the market opens we will wait for price to move below 1.9833 and without touching 1.9819, if price retrace to R1, then we enter at R1.  
  
1 hr PP = 1.9821 and R1 = 1.9829. so we wait for market to retrace below 1.9829 and then without touching 1.9821 when price comes back to R1 we enter.   
  
so those are the trades i see for the 4 hr and 1 hr. my question now is what happens when we refresh and those values for PP and R1 change, do we keep referencing our old values or just abandon everything and look at the new numbers? how do we react to the new values?   
  
thanks

  * [#180](/thread/post/1552066#post1552066 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 22, 2007 4:59pm  Aug 22, 2007 4:59pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41068_4.gif) Olaha](olaha)

  * | Joined Jun 2007  | Status: Leading Trader | [399 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41068)

Yes that is correct... good example but look back at the figure. Enter at 1.9840 and exit at 1.9849... just about 9 pips. That is not worth to take. This is westing time to trade. Try look for a big move, about 20 to 40 pips.  
Sometimes even 1 hr pivot give about 20-60 pips. That is the sign that the market is active. If the pivot figure is small is mean that the market is slow. Take note of this.

No...we have to follow the new target only.   
  
Let say you already entered buy at R1. The next hr.. the PP change than you just need to update you take profit level to the new figure. If you happy with the earlier target than leave it. But the SL you should follow the new PP levels.

In this case is different... this is the news release.  
Is not advisable to take this trade for those new to trading.  
I like to use 30 second and 1 minute chart to see the retracement during the news release. The price also retrace above the pivot for daily, 4 hrs and hourly. That is great...

  * [#226](/thread/post/1553234#post1553234 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 23, 2007 3:15am  Aug 23, 2007 3:15am 

  * [ S-Deuce](s-deuce)

  * | Joined Jul 2007  | Status: Trader | [75 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=42853)

Olaha, question - I was just watching the graphs. Here is what happened...  
  
4 hour pivot = 1.9869  
R1 = 1.9901  
R2 = 1.9936  
R3 = 1.9968  
  
Range = 67 (20/20/20/7)  
  
Price hit R1 and then retraced to 1.9877. Then price rallied back up and broke through R1 and took profit at 20 pips, then adjusted stop loss to 5 above R1 (1.9906). Then the market fell and took out my stop loss and fell to a low of 1.9891 (below R1). Price then rallied again and took out R1 and went to a current High of 1.9923 .  
  
My question is... Since it fell back below R1 after taking me out, at break even + 20 pips that I locked, should I have entered back when it rallied up past R1 and done the same thing? - All the pivot levels were the same, none had changed. 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

  * [#227](/thread/post/1553971#post1553971 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 23, 2007 12:58pm  Aug 23, 2007 12:58pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41068_4.gif) Olaha](olaha)

  * | Joined Jun 2007  | Status: Leading Trader | [399 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41068)

Yes you can do that, as long the price doesn't retrace back at pivot level.  
You can take again at R1 but just becareful bcoz sometimes the price can reverse crazy. Sometimes that happen. Take note of this.  
It's happen to me a few times. Some can be a good move.. big range.  
If this happen, look back at news release. Sometimes, this happen bcoz of Oil price adjustment or some speech happen. Read as much news as possible. Update yourself. Just be aware what happening around the world. Esp. for US matters.

Do you know that sometimes bcoz of you browser load your data very slow, you could missing some data. I don't know why you can't see the cross.  
  
Actually I place an order. Once the price test the R1, then retrace... I place an order immediately. So I get that price. If.. in case the price hit the pivot... I will cancel the order. That's why I get the price.  
  
Next time, I will take the picture where I entered.

It's depend on your spread my dear... some broker give up to 4 pips spread...  
  
my spread only 2.5..  
  
So if the price ASK 1.9975, so my BID 1.9977.  
  
But if your spread is 4,  
So you will get Bid 1.9979

  * [#302](/thread/post/1557862#post1557862 "Post Permalink")

  * Aug 25, 2007 2:35am  Aug 25, 2007 2:35am 

  * [ leo221](leo221)

  * | Joined Apr 2007  | Status: Trader | [48 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=37610)

Once we know when is the best time to trade, we should know what is the trend for the day. The easy way to find the direction of the trend for the days is using the Pivot Point (PP). If the opening price is above the PP means Bullish. If the opening price is below the PP means Bearish.  
  
  
hi olaha:  
in this you said the ''open price''.it mean what time is price?  
thx

Yes that was a good system but the this pivot more accurate and can help me to make a good trade with discipline.   
  
Pivot system give me more trade rather than the previous system.  
  
In my platform.. they name it as Full Stochastic 5,3,3  
In my system, I have Full, Fast and Slow Stochastic.  
If you use [Oanda](/brokers/oanda "View OANDA Broker Profile") broker, you will see this.  
I don't know about others.

  * Aug 28, 2007 3:19pm  Aug 28, 2007 3:19pm 

  * [ Rodrigo](rodrigo)

  * | Joined Aug 2007  | Status: Trader | [34 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=45904)

Hi Olaha,  
  
Thank you. OK so it is if full stochastic. Yesterday I played with your system and I made some pips on GBP/USD and GBP/JPY. I hope that it was not just a coincidence ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1). I hope that it was because I followed all the rules.  
So the price was below daily PP, 4hPP and 1hPP so I expected that the price would go down. I was waiting for the moment when the price would reach the first 4 hour support (4hS1). When it happened the price stopped there for a moment and returned toward 4hPP. It did not reach the 4hPP so it was a good sign that it would go back to 4hS1.  
The price was moving up and down between the 4hS1 and a halfway to 4hPP (did not touch the 4hPP). I observed the Stoch 5,3,3 on 15 M chart. Both curves %K and %D crossed first (somewhere above 50) and then 5 EMA crossed the Stochastic but first it crossed the %K. Was it OK? If the EMA crosses the %K can it be considered as a confirmation?   
Then the price hit the 4hS1 again and when it continued to 4hS2 I entered the trade.  
Did I do it right? In a case like this does the stochastic 5,3,3 have to cross above 50 and go down on 15M chart? Does the stochastic 14,3,3 on 1h chart do the same or it does not matter? And is it enough if the EMA crosses the %K only? This is one thing I am not quite sure about.   
  
Rodrigo.

Seems... U understand the system.   
  
Actually... we don't have really consent on the technical indicator.  
The most important is the Pivot and the money management.  
The indicator is came at last.  
I use the indicator is for confirmation.  
I enter and exit the trade according to the Pivot only.  
For confirmation, than I look at the stochastic for retracement.  
For you all information, Technical analysis is legging indicator.  
So don't focus so much about it.  
Don't worry about where the line cross and etc.  
You can use the standard studies how to use the stochastic.  
  
One thing that you miss is where to enter.  
You should enter at S1 (after the retracement below the PP, than u should place an order at S1, and take profit at S3).  
  
Don't forget about the money management.  
  
My consent is money management.  
If you master on this, you can see the different on your trading style.

I understand, you work until 5 or 6 pm, is difficult to arrange.  
Try to understand the concept and rule.  
Than try to ask me question. I will try to answer the next day.  
After you understand than you start trade by yourself.  
I believe you can do that.

  * | Joined Jun 2007  | Status: Leading Trader | [399 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41068)

We have to use daily pivot to know the major direction.  
For daily pivot, show bearish  
The price move below PP.  
During 6 GMT, the price below pivot for 4hr/1hr (Bearish)  
After 8-10 GMT, the price above pivot for 4hr/1r (Bullish)

#  [](/thread/38542-pivot-point-with-money-management-strategy)Pivot Point with Money Management Strategy 

  * 

  * [#421](/thread/post/1609986#post1609986 "Post Permalink")

  * Sep 25, 2007 4:44pm  Sep 25, 2007 4:44pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41068_4.gif) Olaha](olaha)

  * | Joined Jun 2007  | Status: Leading Trader | [399 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41068)

Is very easy system to follow actually.  
  
If the price above the pivot- bullish,  
If the price below the pivot - bearish,  
  
The entry strategy is;  
For buy:  
Let the price test the R1 first for buy, after the price retrace, make sure the price retrace above the Pivot. If the price back to R1, than we enter buy.  
  
For sell:  
Let the price test the S1 first for sell, after the price retrace, make sure the price retrace below the Pivot. If the price back to S1, than we enter sell.  
  
The daily, 4 hrs, hourly pivot is very important.  
Normally.. I will use the hourly and 4 hr pivot for short-term entry.  
To get a major direction- use daily pivot.  
  
The range from R1-3 and S1-3, must be on big range.  
Is around 30 - 100. If this happen... we can start plan,   
how much lots you want to enter.  
  
Don't worry... soon latter...you will know how to use this system.  
  
Good Luck!

  * Oct 5, 2007 11:26am  Oct 5, 2007 11:26am 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41068_4.gif) Olaha](olaha)

  * | Joined Jun 2007  | Status: Leading Trader | [399 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41068)

Look for the attachment.  
  
  
Additional rule;  
**_To find the right price._**  
Before we calculate a pivot point, we should know to identify the right price to take. Look for valid bar/candlestick.   
  
**_The valid bar/candlestick is ;_**  
For Bullish - close price higher-high,  
For Bearish - close price lower-low.  
  
**Notes: Use Daily/Weekly/Monthly chart. 

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

  * | Joined Mar 2007  | Status: Trader | [606 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=35717)

Are you guys still looking for pivot calculators? They're all over the place. The generic floor pivots formula is:  
  
H = previous high  
L = previous low  
C = previous close  
  
P = (H+L+C)/3  
R1 = (2*P)-L;  
S1 = (2*P)-H;  
R2 = P + H - L;  
S2 = P - H - L;  
R3 = (2*P) + (H - (2*L));  
S3 = (2*P) - ((2*H)-L);   
  
This applies for any periods, including hourly, 4-hr, 12-hr, daily, 5 min, whatever.  
  
Just get an indicator and plug in the formulas and you're good to go. I could do this in 5 minutes with the indicators I have here. Good luck and I hope this helps! 

[0 ](javascript:void\(0\);) [0 ](javascript:void\(0\);)

I think..some of you don't know that Pivot Point has a few types of calculation formula. There are; PP Clasic, PP Woodie's, PP Camarilla, and PP DeMark's.  
  
I find that PP Camarilla one of the tools that help on target projection.  
  
Who's interested to experimenting and adventuring... have a look at this website;..

For those who confuse taking HLC price,  
you can use HLC price from AF.  
For the Current Open Price,   
look for at 6pm EST at current Day.  
  
To calculate PP level for HLC.. we use previous day,  
for open price.. we use on the current day.  
  
I hope you all understand this.  
  
Wish you all the best..

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar41068_4.gif) Olaha](olaha)

  * | Joined Jun 2007  | Status: Leading Trader | [399 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=41068)

Hi Dagoods, Sorry... take a long time to reply... I've been away from this forum for a such long time. Anywhere.. about the system that I suggested. The rules as follow; For Buy: 1). For Bullish trend - The price must be above daily and 1 hr Pivot Point. 2). When 1 hr pivot point move upward to a new level, move higher than the previous pivot hour, this is good signal entry for buy. 3). For confirmation entry, we have to get the second candle confirmation as a bullish candle or wait for new Retracement at above new pivot point. 4). All setting is in 15 minutes chart. For Sell: (Just reverse the Buy signal) For target level- we can use R1,R2,R3 or according to our own money management. Hope this will help you to understand. I try to make it simple as possible.
